proc sort data=mike.drink_rep1;
by _imputation_;
run;
proc surveyphreg data=mike.drink_rep1;
class edlevel(param=ref ref='3') race(param=ref ref='1') married(param=ref ref='1')  
smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms1;
run;
proc print data=parms1;
run;
data parmsclass1;
set parms1;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc print data=parmsclass1;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass1;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass1;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel;
by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink1;
run;
proc print data=m3_cox_drink1;
run;

if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;

by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink27;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms154;
run;
data parmsclass154;
set parms154;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass154 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass154;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink154;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms172;
run;
data parmsclass172;
set parms172;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass172 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass172;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink172;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms190;
run;
data parmsclass190;
set parms190;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass190 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass190;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink190;
run;

class edlevel(param=ref ref='3') race(param=ref ref='1') married(param=ref ref='1')  
smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms208;
run;
data parmsclass208;
set parms208;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass208 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass208;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink208;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms226;
run;
data parmsclass226;
set parms226;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass226 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass226;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink226;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms244;
run;
data parmsclass244;
set parms244;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass244 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass244;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink244;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms262;
run;
data parmsclass262;
set parms262;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass262 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass262;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink262;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms280;
run;
data parmsclass280;
set parms280;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass280 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass280;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink280;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms298;
run;
data parmsclass298;
set parms298;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass298 ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass298;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink298;
run;

data mike.m3_cox_drink_c;
set m3_cox_drink201-m3_cox_drink300;
run;

proc print data=mike.m3_cox_drink_c (obs=10);
run;

data f;
set mike.m3_cox_drink_c;
where domain='flag=1';
run;
proc sort data=f;
by edlevel;
run;
proc means data=f mean median min max;
var estimate;
by edlevel;
run;

class edlevel(param=ref ref='3') race(param=ref ref='1') married(param=ref ref='1')  
smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms352;
run;
data parmsclass352;
set parms352;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass352   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass352;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink352;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms370;
run;
data parmsclass370;
set parms370;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass370   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass370;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink370;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms388;
run;
data parmsclass388;
set parms388;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass388   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass388;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink388;
run;

class edlevel(param=ref ref='3') race(param=ref ref='1') married(param=ref ref='1')  
smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms406;
run;
data parmsclass406;
set parms406;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass406   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass406;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink406;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms424;
run;
data parmsclass424;
set parms424;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass424   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass424;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink424;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms442;
run;
data parmsclass442;
set parms442;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass442   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass442;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink442;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms460;
run;
data parmsclass460;
set parms460;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass460   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass460;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink460;
run;

smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms478;
run;
data parmsclass478;
set parms478;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass478   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass478;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink478;
run;

proc surveyphreg data=mike.drink_rep496;
class edlevel(param=ref ref='3') race(param=ref ref='1') married(param=ref ref='1')  
smoke_4cat(param=ref ref='4') alcohol_cat(param=ref ref='1') bmi_cat(param=ref ref='2') 
chf(param=ref ref='0') cva(param=ref ref='0') copd(param=ref ref='0') ckd(param=ref ref='0')
cancer(param=ref ref='0') diab(param=ref ref='0') highbp(param=ref ref='0')
ami(param=ref ref='0') agecat(param=ref ref='1');
model agedur*dead(0)=agecat race married edlevel alcohol_cat smoke_4cat ami diab highbp cva chf ckd copd cancer
bmi_cat /entry=age;
stratum stratum6;
cluster psu6;
weight wtpfex6;
domain flag;
by _imputation_;
ods output parameterestimates=parms496;
run;
data parmsclass496;
set parms496;
if scan(parameter,1)='edlevel' then do;
effect='edlevel';
edlevel=scan(parameter,2,' ');
end;
run;
proc sort data=parmsclass496   ;
by domain;
run;
proc mianalyze parms(classvar=full)=parmsclass496;
class edlevel;
modeleffects edlevel; by domain;
ods output parameterestimates=m3_cox_drink496;
run;



proc sort data=mike.drink_rep497;
by _imputation_;

data mike.m3_cox_drink_e;
set m3_cox_drink401-m3_cox_drink500;
run;


data mike.m3_cox_drink;
set mike.m3_cox_drink_a mike.m3_cox_drink_b mike.m3_cox_drink_c
mike.m3_cox_drink_d mike.m3_cox_drink_e;
run;

proc print data=mike.m3_cox_drink (obs=20);
run;


data f;
set mike.m3_cox_drink;
if domain='flag=1';
run;

proc sort data=f;
by edlevel;
run;

proc means data=f n mean median min p25 p75 max;
var estimate;
by edlevel;
run;
